DECLARES IV THERAPY TRAINING NOT A REQUIREMENT FOR EMPLOYMENT!',  (Nov 19, 2016) In an announcement posted in the Philippine Star, the Board of Nursing (BON', ...', ) has declared the removal of IV Therapy trainings as pre-employment requirements for nurses through BON Resolution No.38 series of 2016',  Here are the salient points of said resolution:',  ~ IV therapy training SHALL NOT BE REQUIRED for employment or promotion.', u" ~ However, healthcare institutions MAY employ a test to verify the level of the nurse's or skills on intravenous therapy prior to hiring.",  ~ If the nurse demonstrates BASIC COMPETENCE in IV therapy, no further training shall be required of the nurse.',  ~ If the nurse does not demonstrate basic competence in IV therapy, the healthcare institution SHALL PROVIDE intravenous therapy training to as an "in-service training program" AT NO EXPENSE TO THE NURSE, as per BON Resolution 31 s.2015',  ~ ALL IV therapy training programs should be accredited under the Continuing Professional Development (CPD) Council for Nursing, and all accredited providers shall issue certificates which reflect said CPD Units.',  ~ Board Resolution No 08, s of 1994 and all other issuances or parts thereof inconsistent with this Resolution are hereby repealed or amended accordingly.',  (Note) Non-compliance to BON resolutions and guidelines shall be punishable under RA 9173, the Revised Penal Code, the civil code, and other applicable laws.',  Link to BON Resolution No.38 series of 2016:',  ', DECLARES IV THERAPY TRAINING NOT A REQUIREMENT FOR EMPLOYMENT!',  (Nov 19, 2016) In an announcement posted in the Philippine Star, the Board of Nursing (BON', ...', ) has declared the removal of IV Therapy trainings as pre-employment requirements for nurses through BON Resolution No.38 series of 2016',  Here are the salient points of said resolution:',  ~ IV therapy training SHALL NOT BE REQUIRED for employment or promotion.', u" ~ However, healthcare institutions MAY employ a test to verify the level of the nurse's or skills on intravenous therapy prior to hiring.",  ~ If the nurse demonstrates BASIC COMPETENCE in IV therapy, no further training shall be required of the nurse.',  ~ If the nurse does not demonstrate basic competence in IV therapy, the healthcare institution SHALL PROVIDE intravenous therapy training to as an "in-service training program" AT NO EXPENSE TO THE NURSE, as per BON Resolution 31 s.2015',  ~ ALL IV therapy training programs should be accredited under the Continuing Professional Development (CPD) Council for Nursing, and all accredited providers shall issue certificates which reflect said CPD Units.',  ~ Board Resolution No 08, s of 1994 and all other issuances or parts thereof inconsistent with this Resolution are hereby repealed or amended accordingly.',  (Note) Non-compliance to BON resolutions and guidelines shall be punishable under RA 9173, the Revised Penal Code, the civil code, and other applicable laws.',  Link to BON Resolution No.38 series of 2016:',  ',
